| Walant yiwen n usekṛani yeẓẓel deg webrid. |
| Waqil d lawan ad s-d-aɣeɣ takeṛṛust i mmi. |
| Waw! Ad as-tinid aql-aɣ deg umtiweg niḍen. |
| Wehmeɣ imi ay tugi assumer igerrzen am wa. |
| Wellah ma ẓṛiɣ ma yella ad d-iṛuḥ neɣ xaṭi |
| Weltma attan deg yiseggasen-nnes n simraw. |
| Weltma tessewway-aɣ-d isafaren d iẓidanen. |
| Weltma-s tezdeɣ ed wergaz-nnes deg Kanada. |
| Werɛad ur as-fkiɣ ara i wayis-inu ad isew. |
| Werɛad ur d-iban anwa ay yuran tabṛat-nni. |

| Werɛad ur tessin ara ad tenheṛ tasnasɣalt. |
| Werɛad ur tezmir ara ad tenheṛ tasnasɣalt. |
| Werǧin ad alseɣ ad awen-d-ssiwleɣ ɣef Tom. |
| Werǧin ad ɛawdeɣ ad ak-d-ssiwleɣ ɣef waya. |
| Werǧin ad ɛawdeɣ ad am-d-ssiwleɣ ɣef waya. |
| Werǧin ad ɛawdeɣ ad ɣliɣ deg tuccḍa am ta. |
| Werǧin i yi-yennul uqcic alarmi d ass-nni. |

| Werǧin teẓri tajujet yeqquren anect-a akk. |
| Werǧin yessared tafekka-s |  yuɣal d amerku. |
| Werǧin yeẓri tajujet yeqquren anect-a akk. |
| Werǧin ẓrint tajujet yeqquren anect-a akk. |
| Werjin ad ɛawdeɣ ad kem-jjeɣ i yiman-nnem. |
| Werjin ad tebɣu ad tɛawed ad tezdeɣ dinna. |
| Werjin cniɣ s tefṛensist armi d iḍ yezrin. |
| Werjin ihenna seg wasmi ay yemmut memmi-s. |
| Werjin terni teẓra baba-s seg tikkelt-nni. |
| Werjin ttiliɣ deg wexxam deg wass n Lḥedd. |
| Werjin yettaḍsa mi ara as-d-ḥkuɣ taseḍsut. |
| Wid i yugin ad ttwazeɣnen ur ttnegmun ara. |
| Wid i yugin azɣan ur tteddun ara ɣer sdat. |
| Wid iḥemmelen taqbaylit |  aten-aya ad asen! |
| Wid s tidet snulfuyen-d amezruy d igduden. |
| Wid ur iqebblen ara azɣan ur ttneflin ara. |
| Wihin inu. Ur ẓriɣ anda-t win-nnes nettat. |
| Win d argaz yewɛeṛ ad iqerreb ɣer-s yiwen. |
| Win d-yesɛan akluc |  iṛebbi-t i yiman-nnes. |
| Win i iɣurr Cciṭan |  ad iṛuḥ ad yenbec Tom. |
| Win ifehmen ad issefhem wid ur nefhim ara. |
| Win iqqsen izerman ittuggad ula d iseqqan. |
| Win ur nessin tussna |  yettarra-tt ar ddin. |
| Win ur nxeddem |  ur yesɛi ar azref ad yečč. |
| Win yebɣan ad yečč lesfenǧ |  iḍher-ak amek. |
| Win yebɣan kra |  yekkat i wakken ad t-yaweḍ |
| Win yeččan cciṭan ilaq ad yečč acciwen-is. |
| Win yeččan tixsi |  meqqaṛ ad d-yerr taduḍt. |
| Win yessnen ad yargu yettaweḍ ayen yelhan. |
| Winna d amdan aydeg tzemred ad tged laman. |
| Winna d amdan aydeg tzemreḍ ad tgeḍ laman. |
| Winna yeḥwaǧ tiyita s ufḍis ar gar wallen. |
| Wissen acḥal n wakud ay nḍeyyeɛ ar imir-a. |

| Wteɣ acḥal n tsaɛtin akken ad t-ssizedgeɣ. |

| Wwḍeɣ s axxam cwiṭ kan deffir ttnac n yiḍ. |
| Xeddmeɣ yal ass s lḥif deg yiwen n usensu. |

| Ya d kecc ay yeccḍen |  ya d ameddakel-nnek. |
| Yal ass d accetkti |  kker ad tnadiḍ ixeddim |
